throughout its core using three main patterns:\\n\\n## 1. Primordials System (lib/internal/per_context/primordials.js)\\n\\nThe central defense is the **primordials** mechanism. This file captures all built-in JS methods before any user code can tamper with them. Key anti-prototype-pollution exports:\\n\\n- **`ObjectCreate`**, **`ObjectFreeze`**, **`ObjectSetPrototypeOf`**, **`ObjectGetPrototypeOf`** — Safe wrappers for Object methods\\n- **`ObjectHasOwn`** / **`ObjectPrototypeHasOwnProperty`** — Safe own-property checks that bypass inherited `hasOwnProperty` on the prototype chain\\n- **`ObjectDefineProperty`** / **`ObjectDefineProperties`** — Safe property definition bypassing prototype setters\\n- **`makeSafe(unsafe, safe)`** — Creates null-prototype subclasses of Map, Set, WeakMap, WeakSet, WeakRef, etc. via `ObjectSetPrototypeOf(safe.prototype, null)` + `ObjectFreeze(safe.prototype)` + `ObjectFreeze(safe)`, exported as **`SafeMap`**, **`SafeSet`**, **`SafeWeakMap`**, **`SafeWeakSet`**, **`SafeWeakRef`**, **`SafeFinalizationRegistry`**\\n- **`createSafeIterator`** — Produces iterator classes with null prototypes\\n- **`hardenRegExp`** — Strips prototype-accessible flags from RegExp to prevent RegExp pollution\\n- **`uncurryThis`** / **`applyBind`** — Prevents prototype-chain lookups for `Function.prototype.call/apply`\\n- At the end, `ObjectSetPrototypeOf(primordials, null)` and `ObjectFreeze(primordials)` harden the primordials object itself\\n\\n## 2. Intrinsics Freezing (lib/internal/freeze_intrinsics.js)\\n\\nAdapted from Google Caja/SES, this module deep-freezes all JS intrinsics at startup:\\n- **`deepFreeze(root)`** — Transitively freezes all objects reachable from a root, preventing prototype chain extension\\n- **`enableDerivedOverride`** / **`enableDerivedOverrides`** — Converts data properties to accessor properties to allow subclass override while keeping the frozen prototype tamper-proof\\n- Uses `ObjectPrototypeHasOwnProperty` throughout to safely check descriptors\\n\\n## 3. Core Utility Safe Patterns (lib/internal/util.js)\\n\\n- **`kEmptyObject`** — `ObjectFreeze({ __proto__: null })` — a frozen null-prototype empty object used as a safe default for options parameters across the codebase\\n- **`kEnumerableProperty`** — A null-prototype property descriptor template\\n- **`filterOwnProperties(source, keys)`** — Copies only own properties using `ObjectPrototypeHasOwnProperty`, returning a `{ __proto__: null }` result object\\n- **`setOwnProperty(obj, key, value)`** — Uses `ObjectDefineProperty` to set a property ignoring prototype chain setters\\n\\n## 4. Object.create(null) / {__proto__: null} for Data Objects\\n\\nThroughout the codebase, null-prototype objects are used for data dictionaries to prevent prototype pollution:\\n- **`lib/querystring.js`** `parse()`: `const obj = { __proto__: null }` — critical for preventing `__proto__`, `constructor`, and `toString` keys from polluting Object.prototype when parsing user-supplied query strings\\n- **`lib/internal/modules/cjs/loader.js`**: `Module._cache`, `Module._pathCache`, `Module._extensions`, `relativeResolveCache` all use `{ __proto__: null }` to prevent }` to neutralize any `__proto__` keys\\n- **`lib/internal/source_map/source_map.js`**, **`lib/internal/error_serdes.js`**, **`lib/internal/encoding/single-byte.js`**: Lookup tables stored as `{ __proto__: null }` objects\\n\\n## 5. hasOwnProperty Safe Checks\\n\\nFiles that use `ObjectHasOwn` or `ObjectPrototypeHasOwnProperty` (primordial-safe forms) rather than the prototype-accessible `.hasOwnProperty()` method:\\n- `lib/internal/bootstrap/realm.js` — defines `getOwn()` using `ObjectPrototypeHasOwnProperty`\\n- `lib/internal/util/parse_args/utils.js` — defines `objectGetOwn()` throughout its core using three main patterns:\\n\\n## 1. Primordials System (lib/internal/per_context/primordials.js)\\n\\nThe central defense is the **primordials** mechanism. This file captures all built-in JS methods before any user code can tamper with them. Key anti-prototype-pollution exports:\\n\\n- **`ObjectCreate`**, **`ObjectFreeze`**, **`ObjectSetPrototypeOf`**, **`ObjectGetPrototypeOf`** — Safe wrappers for Object methods\\n- **`ObjectHasOwn`** / **`ObjectPrototypeHasOwnProperty`** — Safe own-property checks that bypass inherited `hasOwnProperty` on the prototype chain\\n- **`ObjectDefineProperty`** / **`ObjectDefineProperties`** — Safe property definition bypassing prototype setters\\n- **`makeSafe(unsafe, safe)`** — Creates null-prototype subclasses of Map, Set, WeakMap, WeakSet, WeakRef, etc. via `ObjectSetPrototypeOf(safe.prototype, null)` + `ObjectFreeze(safe.prototype)` + `ObjectFreeze(safe)`, exported as **`SafeMap`**, **`SafeSet`**, **`SafeWeakMap`**, **`SafeWeakSet`**, **`SafeWeakRef`**, **`SafeFinalizationRegistry`**\\n- **`createSafeIterator`** — Produces iterator classes with null prototypes\\n- **`hardenRegExp`** — Strips prototype-accessible flags from RegExp to prevent RegExp pollution\\n- **`uncurryThis`** / **`applyBind`** — Prevents prototype-chain lookups for `Function.prototype.call/apply`\\n- At the end, `ObjectSetPrototypeOf(primordials, null)` and `ObjectFreeze(primordials)` harden the primordials object itself\\n\\n## 2. Intrinsics Freezing (lib/internal/freeze_intrinsics.js)\\n\\nAdapted from Google Caja/SES, this module deep-freezes all JS intrinsics at startup:\\n- **`deepFreeze(root)`** — Transitively freezes all objects reachable from a root, preventing prototype chain extension\\n- **`enableDerivedOverride`** / **`enableDerivedOverrides`** — Converts data properties to accessor properties to allow subclass override while keeping the frozen prototype tamper-proof\\n- Uses `ObjectPrototypeHasOwnProperty` throughout to safely check descriptors\\n\\n## 3. Core Utility Safe Patterns (lib/internal/util.js)\\n\\n- **`kEmptyObject`** — `ObjectFreeze({ __proto__: null })` — a frozen null-prototype empty object used as a safe default for options parameters across the codebase\\n- **`kEnumerableProperty`** — A null-prototype property descriptor template\\n- **`filterOwnProperties(source, keys)`** — Copies only own properties using `ObjectPrototypeHasOwnProperty`, returning a `{ __proto__: null }` result object\\n- **`setOwnProperty(obj, key, value)`** — Uses `ObjectDefineProperty` to set a property ignoring prototype chain setters\\n\\n## 4. Object.create(null) / {__proto__: null} for Data Objects\\n\\nThroughout the codebase, null-prototype objects are used for data dictionaries to prevent prototype pollution:\\n- **`lib/querystring.js`** `parse()`: `const obj = { __proto__: null }` — critical for preventing `__proto__`, `constructor`, and `toString` keys from polluting Object.prototype when parsing user-supplied query strings\\n- **`lib/internal/modules/cjs/loader.js`**: `Module._cache`, `Module._pathCache`, `Module._extensions`, `relativeResolveCache` all use `{ __proto__: null }` to prevent pollution via malicious module names\\n- **`lib/internal/http2/compat.js`**: HTTP/2 headers initialized with `{ __proto__: null }` (explicitly noted in comment as intentional, unlike HTTP/1 which uses plain objects for compatibility)\\n- **`lib/_http_agent.js`** / **`lib/_http_client.js`** / **`lib/child_process.js`** / **`lib/https.js`**: Options objects spread with `{ __proto__: null, ...options }` to neutralize any `__proto__` keys\\n- **`lib/internal/source_map/source_map.js`**, **`lib/internal/error_serdes.js`**, **`lib/internal/encoding/single-byte.js`**: Lookup tables stored as `{ __proto__: null }` objects\\n\\n## 5. hasOwnProperty Safe Checks\\n\\nFiles that use `ObjectHasOwn` or `ObjectPrototypeHasOwnProperty` (primordial-safe forms) rather than the prototype-accessible `.hasOwnProperty()` method:\\n- `lib/internal/bootstrap/realm.js` — defines `getOwn()` using `ObjectPrototypeHasOwnProperty`\\n- `lib/internal/util/parse_args/utils.js` — defines `objectGetOwn()` using `ObjectHasOwn`\\n- `lib/internal/util/parse_args/parse_args.js` — uses `ObjectHasOwn` throughout for safe config access\\n- `lib/internal/crypto/util.js`, `lib/internal/crypto/webidl.js` — safe algorithm registry checks\\n- `lib/internal/console/constructor.js`, `lib/internal/cli_table.js` — safe own-property iteration\\n- `lib/internal/util/comparisons.js`, `lib/internal/util/inspect.js` — safe deep-equality and inspection\\n- `lib/cluster.js`, `lib/buffer.js`, `lib/child_process.js`, `lib/_http_outgoing.js` — various own-property checks\\n\\n## 6. Safe Merge/Assign Patterns\\n\\nThe `{ __proto__: null, ...spread }` pattern is used in place of plain `Object.assign()` to neutralize `__proto__` in spread sources:\\n- `lib/_http_agent.js`: `options = { __proto__: null, ...options, ...this.options }`\\n- `lib/child_process.js`: `options = { __proto__: null, ...options }`\\n- `lib/https.js`: `options = { __proto__: null, ...options }`\\n- `lib/internal/per_context/primordials.js`: property descriptors use `{ __proto__: null, ...desc }` when copying\\n\\nThe `kEmptyObject` constant (frozen null-prototype `{}`) is imported in over 60 files as a safe default parameter to prevent options object prototype pollution.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
